creations-chat 2022-10-06 10:18:11 Ok, pro tip. Dont try and link plane crazy to irl, its nothing like that, building mechanics are NOT like how you would actually build a plane. After all these steps are complete, you are now a plane crazy pro. It is best if you have someone to teach you in game.
